  <script>
   (function() {
        var BBCL = (window.BBCL = window.BBCL || {})
        var mixins = (BBCL.mixins = BBCL.mixins || [])

        mixins.push({
            methods: {
                headerOpenRadio(ciudad) {
                    event.preventDefault()
                    var h=520,
                    i=320,
                    k=screen.width,
                    j=screen.height,
                    b=Math.round(k/2-h/2),c=0;j>i&&(c=Math.round(j/2-i/2));
                    var url = '//vivo.biobiochile.cl/player/?radio=' + ciudad;
                    window.open(url, "_blank", 'width='+i+',height='+h+',left='+b+',top=100');
                }
            }
        })
    })()
  </script>
  <script>
   //Variables Necesarias
        // var signInButton = document.getElementById('sign-in');
    var subscribeText = "<i class='fa fa-bell bell' aria-hidden='true'></i> Activar notificaciones";
    var unsubscribeText = "<i class='fa fa-bell bell' aria-hidden='true'></i> Desactivar notificaciones";

    //Checkea permisos y asigna texto al boton
    function subscribeButton(){
        var permission = Notification.permission;
        if(permission !== "denied") {
            document.getElementById("sign-in").removeAttribute("hidden");
            console.log("Permission:" + permission);
            if(permission == "granted"){
                OneSignal.push(function() {
                    OneSignal.isPushNotificationsEnabled(function(isEnabled) {
                        if (isEnabled){
                            document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = unsubscribeText;
                        }
                        else{
                            document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = subscribeText;
                        }
                    })
                });
            }
            else{
                document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = subscribeText;
            }
        }
    };
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', subscribeButton())

    //Funciones del boton
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        document.getElementById("sign-in").addEventListener('click', function(){
            var permission = Notification.permission;
            if(permission === "default") {
                OneSignal.push(function() {
                    OneSignal.showNativePrompt();
                });
            }
            if(permission === "granted") {
                OneSignal.isPushNotificationsEnabled(function(isEnabled) {
                    if (isEnabled){
                        console.log("Push notifications were enabled and now are disabled!");
                        OneSignal.setSubscription(false);
                        document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = subscribeText;

                    }else{
                        console.log("Push notifications were disabled and now are enabled!");
                        OneSignal.setSubscription(true);
                        document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = unsubscribeText;
                    }
                });
            }
        }, false)
    })

    //Escucha cambios en los permisos del navegador
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        OneSignal.push(function() {
            OneSignal.on('notificationPermissionChange', function(permissionChange) {
                var currentPermission = permissionChange.to;
                if (permissionChange.to === "denied") {
                    document.getElementById("sign-in").setAttribute("hidden", "true");
                    document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = subscribeText;
                }else if (permissionChange.to === "granted"){
                    document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = unsubscribeText;
                }else{
                    document.getElementById("sign-in").innerHTML = subscribeText;
                }
            });
        });
    })
  </script>

   <!-- [/SECTION STREAMING ESCRITORIO] -->
   <script>
    (function () {
		var streamingBox = document.getElementById("streaming-box");
		var streamingIframe = document.getElementById("streaming-iframe");
		var streamingHtmlContainer = document.getElementById(
			"streaming-html-container"
		);
		var lastSrc = "";
		var lastHtml = "";

		// Only work well when parent has one child
		function changeSrc(iframe, src) {
			var parent = iframe.parentNode;
			parent.removeChild(iframe);
			iframe.src = src;
			parent.appendChild(iframe);

			return src;
		}

		function fetch() {
			var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();

			xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
				if (this.readyState == 4) {
					if (this.status == 200) {
						var data = JSON.parse(this.responseText);

						if (data.show && data.src) {
							streamingBox.style.display = "block";

							if (data.src != lastSrc) {
								lastSrc = changeSrc(streamingIframe, data.src);

								if (window.ga) {
									window.ga(
										"send",
										"event",
										"Reproductor Live BBCL",
										"impression"
									);
								}
							}

							if (data.html != lastHtml) {
								lastHtml = data.html;
								streamingHtmlContainer.innerHTML = lastHtml.replace(
									/\[timestamp\]/,
									String(Date.now())
								);
							}
						} else {
							streamingBox.style.display = "none";

							if (lastSrc != "") {
								lastSrc = changeSrc(streamingIframe, "");
							}

							if (lastHtml != "") {
								streamingHtmlContainer.innerHTML = lastHtml = "";
							}
						}
					}
				}
			};

			xhr.open(
				"GET",
				"https://www.biobiochile.cl/static/streaming.json?t=" + Date.now()
			);
			xhr.timeout = 18000;
			xhr.send();
		}

		fetch();
		setInterval(fetch, 20000);
	})();
   </script>

                                        podcasts[1] = aux
                                    }

                                    new Vue({

  <script>
   function sumArray(arr) {
                var sum = 0;
                arr.forEach(function(element){
                    sum = sum + parseInt(element, 10);
                });
                return sum;
            }

            function nDayAverage(n, fechas, cantidades) {
                var avgArr = [];
                var arr = [];
                while (cantidades.length > n) {
                    var values = cantidades.slice(0,7);
                    var avg = (sumArray(values)/7);
                    cantidades = cantidades.slice(1);
                    avgArr.push(avg.toFixed(1));
                }

                avgArr.forEach(function(val,i){
                    arr.push({
                        fecha: fechas[i],
                        cantidad: val
                    })
                })

                return arr;
            }

        (function() {
            moment.locale('es');

            var chart = new Chart(document.querySelector('#chart').getContext('2d'), {

            var BBCL = (window.BBCL = window.BBCL || {})
            var plugins = (BBCL.plugins = BBCL.plugins || [])

            plugins.push(function(Vue, store) {

                store.watch(
                    function(state) {
                        return state.BBCL ? state.BBCL.darkMode : false
                    },
                    function(darkMode) {
                        chart.options.scales.xAxes[0].ticks.fontColor = darkMode ? 'rgba(250, 250, 250, 0.8)' : 'rgba(34, 34, 34, 0.8)'
                        chart.options.scales.yAxes[0].ticks.fontColor = darkMode ? 'rgba(250, 250, 250, 0.8)' : 'rgba(34, 34, 34, 0.8)'
                        chart.data.datasets[0].borderColor = darkMode ? '#FFFFFF' : '#DE0909'
                        chart.data.datasets[0].backgroundColor = darkMode ? 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15)' : 'rgba(222, 9, 9, 0.2)'
                        chart.update()
                    },

                )
            })

            $.getJSON("/static/coronavirus-v3.json", function(data) {
                Chart.defaults.global.defaultFontFamily = "Ubuntu";

                document.getElementById("contagios").innerHTML = '+ ' + data.nuevos_contagios.toLocaleString('pt-EU');
                document.getElementById("total_contagios").innerHTML = data.contagios_totales.toLocaleString('pt-EU');

                document.getElementById("total_fallecidos").innerHTML = data.fallecidos.toLocaleString('pt-EU');

                document.getElementById("segunda_region").innerHTML = data.segunda_region.replace(String.fromCharCode(92), '');
                document.getElementById("segunda_alza").innerHTML = '<i class="fa fa-chevron-up sub3-2-2" aria-hidden="true"></i>' + data.segunda_alza;
                document.getElementById("tercera_region").innerHTML = data.tercera_region.replace(String.fromCharCode(92), '');
                document.getElementById("tercer_alza").innerHTML = '<i class="fa fa-chevron-up sub3-2-2" aria-hidden="true"></i>' + data.tercer_alza;
                document.getElementById("actualizado").innerHTML = 'Actualizado: ' + data.actualizado_dia_mes + ' - ' + data.actualizado_hora;

                data.historial_contagios.forEach(function(element){
                    var date = element.fecha.split('-')
                    element.fecha = new Date(date[0], date[1] - 1, date[2])
                })

                var sortedHistorial = data.historial_contagios.sort(function(a, b){return (b.fecha - a.fecha)}).slice(0,365);

                var sortedDates = [];

                var sortedQties = [];

                sortedHistorial.forEach(function(obj, i){
                    sortedDates.push(moment(obj.fecha, "YYYY-MM-DD").toDate());
                    sortedQties.push(obj.cantidad);
                })

                var sortedAvgHistorial = nDayAverage(7, sortedDates, sortedQties);

                chart.data.labels = sortedAvgHistorial.map(function(item){return item.fecha})
                chart.data.datasets[0].data = sortedAvgHistorial.map(function(item){return item.cantidad})
                chart.canvas.parentNode.style.width = '310px';
                chart.canvas.parentNode.style.height = '140px';
                chart.update()

            });
        })()

                mounted: function() {
                    var cantidadNotasAzar = this.barraNuevaConstitucion.mostrarBanner ? 2 : 3
                    this.barraNuevaConstitucion.notasElegidasAlAzar = this.getMeRandomElements(this.barraNuevaConstitucion.notasParaElegir, cantidadNotasAzar)

                methods: {
                    getMeRandomElements: function(sourceArray, neededElements) {
                        var result = [];
                        var randomIndex = [];
                        for (var i = 0; i < neededElements; i++) {
                            randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random()*sourceArray.length);
                            result.push(sourceArray[randomIndex]);
                            sourceArray.splice(randomIndex, 1);
                        }
                        return result;
                    }
                }

                        fetchSuperTitular: function (context) {
                            Vue.axios(

                            )
                                .then(function (data) {
                                    if (data.data.time > context.state.superTitular.time) {

                        }
                    }
                })

                                title: 'Contagios por región',
                                icon: 'icono0.png'
                            },
                            {
                            url: 'https://www.biobiochile.cl/noticias/ciencia-y-tecnologia/ciencia/2020/03/12/las-claves-del-covid-19-lo-que-debes-saber-sobre-el-virus-que-se-convirtio-en-pandemia-global.shtml',
                            title: 'Lo que debo saber',
                            icon: 'icono1.png'
                            },
                            {
                            url: 'https://www.biobiochile.cl/subsidios/',
                            title: 'Subsidios',
                            icon: 'icono2.png'
                            },
                            {
                            url: 'https://www.biobiochile.cl/noticias/vida-actual/cuerpo-y-mente-sanos/2020/03/06/viajaras-en-bus-6-consejos-para-evitar-el-contagio-con-coronavirus.shtml',
                            title: 'Evitar contagio en viajes',
                            icon: 'icono3.png'
                            },
                            {
                            url: 'https://www.biobiochile.cl/noticias/nacional/chile/2020/03/13/que-deben-hacer-los-trabajadores-en-caso-de-cuarentena-por-coronavirus.shtml',
                            title: 'En caso de cuarentena',
                            icon: 'icono4.png'
                            },
                            {
                            url: 'https://www.biobiochile.cl/noticias/nacional/chile/2020/03/13/segun-sintomas-como-se-diferencia-el-coronavirus-de-la-gripe-comun-y-resfriado.shtml',
                            title: 'Diferencias con gripe',
                            icon: 'icono5.png'
                            },
                            {
                            url: 'https://www.biobiochile.cl/noticias/vida-actual/cuerpo-y-mente-sanos/2020/03/03/conoce-los-sintomas-del-nuevo-coronavirus-covid-19.shtml',
                            title: 'Síntomas',
                            icon: 'icono6.png'
                            },
                        ],
                        lastUpdate: '',
                            infected: 0,
                            new_infected: 0,
                            deceased: 0,
                            new_deceased: 0,
                            recovered: 0,
                            restrictions: [],
                            fetching: false,
                            intervalId: -1
                        }
                    },
                    computed: {
                        marqueeDuration: function() {
                        return this.restrictions.reduce(function(previous, current) {
                            return previous + current.length
                        }, 0) / 3.5
                        }
                    },
                    mounted: function() {
                        this.fetch()
                        this.intervalId = setInterval(this.fetch, 45000)
                    },
                    destroyed: function() {
                        clearInterval(this.intervalId)
                    },
                    methods: {
                        fetch: function() {
                            if(!this.fetching) {
                                this.fetching = true
                                var t = this

                                Vue.axios('https://www.biobiochile.cl/static/coronavirus-v3.json?t=' + Date.now()).then(function(data) {
                                    t.lastUpdate = data.data.actualizado
                                    t.infected = data.data.contagios_totales
                                    t.new_infected = data.data.nuevos_contagios
                                    t.restrictions = data.data.restricciones
                                    t.recovered = data.data.recuperados
                                    t.deceased = data.data.fallecidos
                                    t.new_deceased = data.data.nuevos_fallecidos
                                    t.fetching = false
                                }).catch(function() {
                                    t.fetching = false
                                })
                            }
                        },
                    },
                    filters: {
                        twoDigits: function(x) {
                        return x / 10 < 1 ? '0' + x : String(x)
                        },
                        formatNumber: function(n) {
                            return (+n).toLocaleString('en-US').replace(/,/g, '.')
                        }
                    }
                })
            })

        })()
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
